<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal 2023 Fourth-quarter and Full-year Results and Provides Fiscal 2024 Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Board of Directors Declares Nine Percent Dividend Increase </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Full Year Highlights </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were up 10&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

was up 8&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$4.30 was up 10&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fourth Quarter Highlights </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit of $818&nbsp;million was down 19&nbsp;percent; adjusted operating profit of $889&nbsp;million
effectively matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS of $1.03 was down 24&nbsp;percent; adjusted diluted EPS of $1.12 increased 1&nbsp;percent in
constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (June 28, 2023) &#150;
General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended May&nbsp;28, 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We delivered
excellent results in fiscal 2023, including generating double-digit growth in organic net sales and constant-currency adjusted diluted EPS and exceeding $20&nbsp;billion in annual net sales for the first time in our company&#146;s history,&#148;
said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Led by our Accelerate strategy, our team successfully navigated a highly dynamic operating environment with agility, focus, and resilience.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;As we turn to fiscal 2024, we&#146;ll lean on these same traits to continue to succeed in an evolving business landscape. We&#146;ll
focus on continuing to compete effectively, driving efficiency in our operations, and maintaining our disciplined approach to capital allocation, which we expect to result in financial performance that meets or exceeds each of our key long-term
goals. To underscore our commitment to driving strong returns to General Mills shareholders, our Board approved a nine percent dividend increase effective with the August 2023 payment.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth
and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and
standing for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to
further enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fourth Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 3&nbsp;percent to $5.0&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 5&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price realization
and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume, including a headwind from a reduction in retailer inventory in North America Retail. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 180 basis points to 34.4&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs and
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross margin was up 120 basis points to 35.0&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, including 9&nbsp;percent input cost inflation in the quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $818&nbsp;million was down 19&nbsp;percent, reflecting higher selling, general, and
administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses, higher restructuring charges, and lower gross profit dollars, partially offset by favorable net investment activity. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 16.3&nbsp;percent was down 450 basis points. Adjusted
operating profit of $889&nbsp;million effectively matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels in constant currency, with higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment, offset by higher
adjusted gross profit dollars. Adjusted operating profit margin was down 60 basis points to 17.7&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> of $615&nbsp;million were down 25&nbsp;percent and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was down 24&nbsp;percent to $1.03, driven primarily by lower operating profit. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.12 increased 1&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by lower benefit
plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Full Year Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 6&nbsp;percent to $20.1&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 10&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 110 basis points to 32.6&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs and
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross margin was up 120 basis points to 34.2&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, including 13&nbsp;percent annual input cost inflation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $3.4&nbsp;billion was down 1&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by higher SG&amp;A
expenses and higher restructuring charges, partially offset by gains on divestitures and higher gross profit dollars.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 17.1&nbsp;percent was down 120 basis points. Adjusted operating profit of $3.46&nbsp;billion
increased 8&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment. Adjusted operating profit margin increased
30 basis points to 17.2&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were down 4&nbsp;percent to $2.6&nbsp;billion and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was down 2&nbsp;percent to $4.31, primarily reflecting lower operating profit, a higher effective tax rate, and lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures, partially offset by lower net shares
outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $4.30 was up 10&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, a lower adjusted effective tax rate, and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by lower benefit
plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income and lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following transactions had a significant impact on the comparability of financial results between fiscal 2022 and fiscal 2023: the acquisition of Tyson
Foods&#146; pet treat business in the first quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of the European yogurt business in the third quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of certain international dough businesses in the third and fourth quarters of
fiscal 2022; the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023; and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, fiscal 2023 results included the impact of a voluntary recall on certain international
<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. Unallocated corporate items in fiscal 2023 included an additional
$22&nbsp;million of charges related to product disposals associated with the ice cream recall that were excluded from adjusted operating profit results. The company does not expect a material impact from the ice cream recall beyond fiscal 2023. </P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 2&nbsp;percent to $3.1&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from divestitures, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from unfavorable foreign currency
exchange. Organic net sales increased 5&nbsp;percent. Net sales performance was negatively impacted by a reduction in retailer inventory, with comparable Nielsen-measured retail sales up 10&nbsp;percent in the quarter. Segment operating profit of
$780&nbsp;million was up 2&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit
increase in media investment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, North America Retail segment net sales increased 9&nbsp;percent to $12.66&nbsp;billion,
including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from divestitures and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were up 12&nbsp;percent. Net sales
growth was broad based, including increases of 13&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks, 10&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, and 7&nbsp;percent in U.S. Morning Foods. Constant-currency net sales were up 8&nbsp;percent in Canada. Segment
operating profit of $3.2&nbsp;billion was up 18&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses,
including a double-digit increase in media investment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the Pet segment increased 7&nbsp;percent to $655&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset
by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were also up 7&nbsp;percent. Net sales were up double digits for dry pet food, up high-single digits for pet treats, and down high-single digits for wet pet food. Segment operating profit of $133&nbsp;million
was up 18&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media
investment, and higher other cost of goods sold. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, Pet segment net sales increased 9&nbsp;percent to $2.5&nbsp;billion.
Organic net sales were also up 9&nbsp;percent. Net sales were up double digits for dry pet food and pet treats and were flat for wet pet food. Segment operating profit was down 5&nbsp;percent to $446&nbsp;million, driven primarily by higher input
costs, higher SG&amp;A expenses, and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 7&nbsp;percent to $564&nbsp;million, driven primarily by a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from market index pricing on bakery flour. Segment
operating profit was down 10&nbsp;percent to $72&nbsp;million, driven primarily by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, North America Foodservice net sales increased 19&nbsp;percent to $2.2&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 13&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 14&nbsp;percent to $290&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization
and mix and higher volume, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the International segment were down 1&nbsp;percent to $745&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume, including the impact of the
dough divestitures, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent, led by high-single-digit growth
in Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia and China. Segment operating profit of $67&nbsp;million was down 12&nbsp;percent as reported and down 9&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses,
partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, International net sales were down 16&nbsp;percent to
$2.8&nbsp;billion, driven by lower pound volume, including the impact of the yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by
favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $162&nbsp;million was down 30&nbsp;percent as reported and down 25&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher input costs and
lower volume, including the impacts of the yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter
constant-currency net sales increased 8&nbsp;percent for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) and essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ).
Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures increased 19&nbsp;percent to $23&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix for CPW, partially offset by higher input costs for
CPW and HDJ. For the full year, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $81&nbsp;million compared to $112&nbsp;million a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Full-year
unallocated corporate items totaled $1,033&nbsp;million net expense in fiscal 2023 compared to $403&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT>
valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $621&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to $445&nbsp;million net expense last year, driven primarily by higher compensation and benefits expense,
capability investments, and corporate charitable contributions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded a net $445&nbsp;million <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain on divestitures in fiscal 2023 compared to a net $194&nbsp;million gain a year ago <I>(please see Note 2 below for more information on these items)</I>. Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs
totaled $56&nbsp;million this year compared to a $26&nbsp;million net recovery a year ago <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled
$89&nbsp;million this year compared to $113&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by an increase in interest cost, partially offset by lower amortization of losses and a higher expected return on plan assets. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense in fiscal 2023 totaled $382&nbsp;million compared to $380&nbsp;million
a year ago, with higher interest rates largely offset by lower average long-term debt balances. The effective tax rate for fiscal 2023 was 19.5&nbsp;percent compared to 18.3&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 6 below for more information on
our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was 20.4&nbsp;percent compared to 20.9&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation
and Cash Returns </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $2.8&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2023 compared to $3.3&nbsp;billion a year ago, driven
primarily by changes in inventory and accounts payable. Capital investments of $690&nbsp;million were up 21&nbsp;percent from a year ago. Full-year operating cash flow conversion was 106&nbsp;percent of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings and free cash flow conversion was 80&nbsp;percent of adjusted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. Dividends paid increased 3&nbsp;percent to $1.3&nbsp;billion.
General Mills repurchased approximately 18&nbsp;million shares of common stock in fiscal 2023 for a total of $1.4&nbsp;billion compared to $877&nbsp;million in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding decreased 2&nbsp;percent
to 601&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Dividend Increase </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
General Mills board of directors declared a quarterly dividend of $0.59 per share, payable August&nbsp;1, 2023, to shareholders of record July&nbsp;10, 2023. This represents a 9&nbsp;percent increase from the previous quarterly rate of $0.54 per
share. General Mills and its predecessor company have paid dividends without interruption for 124 years. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2024 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills expects the largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2024 will be the economic health of consumers, the moderating rate of input cost
inflation, and the increasing stability of the supply chain environment. The company expects to drive organic net sales growth in fiscal 2024 through strong marketing, innovation, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-store</FONT> support, and net
price realization generated through its Strategic Revenue Management (SRM) capability, most of which will be carried over from SRM actions taken in fiscal 2023. For the full year, input cost inflation is expected to be 5&nbsp;percent of total cost
of goods sold, driven primarily by labor inflation that continues to impact sourcing, manufacturing, and logistics costs. The company expects to generate HMM cost savings of roughly 4&nbsp;percent of cost of goods sold, compared to 3&nbsp;percent
achieved in fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With these assumptions in mind, General Mills outlined its full-year financial targets for fiscal 2024&sup2;: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales</P></TD>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal year ends on the last Sunday in May. Our India
business is on an April fiscal year end. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we acquired TNT Crust, a manufacturer of high-quality frozen pizza
crusts for regional and national pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $157&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. The
consolidated results of the TNT Crust business are reported in our North America Foodservice segment on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we completed the asset sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle
Family Foods Group for $607&nbsp;million and recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $442&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
fiscal 2022, we sold our European dough businesses and recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain on sale of $30&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we sold our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to
Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for Sodiaal&#146;s interest in our Canadian yogurt business, a modified agreement for the use of <I>Yoplait</I> and <I>Libert&eacute;</I> brands in the United States and Canada, and cash. We recorded a net
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $164&nbsp;million on the sale of these businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of
fiscal 2022, we acquired Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I>, and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer
relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet reporting unit and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2023, we approved restructuring actions to enhance the efficiency of our global supply chain
structure. We expect to incur approximately $52&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and project-related costs related to these actions, of which approximately $35&nbsp;million will be cash. These charges are expected to consist of approximately
$26&nbsp;million of severance and $26&nbsp;million of other costs, primarily $8&nbsp;million of asset impairment and $11&nbsp;million of other asset write-offs. We recognized $26&nbsp;million of severance and $10&nbsp;million of other costs in
fiscal 2023. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2025. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2023, we approved restructuring actions in our
International segment to optimize our H&auml;agen-Dazs shops network. We expect to incur approximately $10&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and project-related costs related to these actions, of which approximately $9&nbsp;million will be cash.
These charges are expected to consist of approximately $6&nbsp;million of severance and $4&nbsp;million of other costs. We recognized $6&nbsp;million of severance and $1&nbsp;million of other costs in fiscal 2023. We expect these actions to be
completed by the end of fiscal 2024. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2022, we approved restructuring actions in the International segment to drive
efficiencies in manufacturing and logistics operations. In connection with these actions, we recorded $15&nbsp;million of restructuring charges, consisting of $8&nbsp;million of severance and $7&nbsp;million of other costs, primarily asset
write-offs. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$74&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023, we recorded a $26&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories compared to a $117&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the fourth quarter of fiscal

and valuation adjustments in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022, we recorded $16&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute;
Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expense totaled

valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories in fiscal 2023, compared to a $133&nbsp;million net decrease in expense last year. We recorded $84&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments and the sale of corporate

<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products. In addition, we recorded $6&nbsp;million of integration costs primarily related to our acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023, compared to $22&nbsp;million of
integration costs related to our acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. In fiscal 2022, we recorded $73&nbsp;million of transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques
SNC, Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses. In addition, we recorded a $22&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item and a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery in fiscal 2022. In addition,
certain compensation and benefits expenses and charitable contributions increased in fiscal 2023 compared to fiscal 2022. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net
sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales
growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd week,
when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in
our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange
(constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding
period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the
average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors because they provide
transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility
in foreign currency exchange markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also, certain measures in this release are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are
either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in management&#146;s judgment, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating
results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2024 outlook for organic net sales growth, constant-currency adjusted operating profit, adjusted diluted EPS, and free
cash flow conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations,
restructuring charges and project-related costs, acquisition transaction and integration costs, acquisitions, divestitures, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. We are not able
to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measures without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a
reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates and commodity prices or the timing or impact of acquisitions, divestitures, and restructuring actions throughout fiscal 2024. The unavailable information
could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2024 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2024, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange
rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and acquisitions and divestitures completed prior to fiscal 2024 to reduce net sales growth by approximately one half of one percent and restructuring charges to total
approximately $15&nbsp;million to $20&nbsp;million. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain (loss), net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023.
Divestitures gain related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Divestiture loss related to the sale of our
Latic&iacute;nios Carolina business in Brazil in fiscal 2021. Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2023. Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of
certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022 and fiscal 2021. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges (recoveries) and

and previously announced actions in fiscal 2023. Restructuring charges for International restructuring actions and net restructuring recoveries for previously announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2022. Restructuring charges for previously
announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2021. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Voluntary recall costs recorded in fiscal 2023 related to certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I>
ice cream products, net of insurance recovery. Product recall adjustment recorded in fiscal 2021 related to a recall in our international Green Giant business in fiscal 2020. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023. Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of
Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Fiscal 2022
transaction costs related primarily to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl, the sale of our European dough businesses, the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side
business, and the acquisition of TNT Crust. Fiscal 2021 transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business.
Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery</U> </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our
adjusted operating profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Diluted EPS and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors
because it is the profitability measure we use to evaluate earnings performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P>

the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Net Sales Growth Rate for Canada Operating Unit on a Constant-currency Basis</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure of our Canada operating unit net sales provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to the underlying
performance for the Canada operating unit within our North America Retail segment by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
